<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Airports">Airports</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=San_Diego_County,_California&amp;action=edit&amp;section=41" title="Edit section: Airports">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/San_Diego_International_Airport" title="San Diego International Airport">Lindbergh Field</a> (San Diego International Airport) (SAN)</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Montgomery_Field" title="Montgomery Field">Montgomery Field</a>, (MYF)</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/McClellan-Palomar_Airport" title="McClellan-Palomar Airport">McClellan-Palomar Airport</a>, (CLD or CRQ) a.k.a. Palomar Airport or Carlsbad Airport</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Gillespie_Field" title="Gillespie Field">Gillespie Field</a>, (SEE) in El Cajon</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Agua_Caliente_Airport" title="Agua Caliente Airport">Agua Caliente Airport</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Borrego_Valley_Airport" title="Borrego Valley Airport">Borrego Valley Airport</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Fallbrook_Community_Airpark" title="Fallbrook Community Airpark">Fallbrook Airport</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Oceanside_Municipal_Airport" title="Oceanside Municipal Airport">Oceanside Municipal Airport</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Ocotillo_Airport" title="Ocotillo Airport">Ocotillo Airport</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Ramona_Airport" title="Ramona Airport">Ramona Airport</a>, (RNM)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Brown_Field_Municipal_Airport" title="Brown Field Municipal Airport">Brown Field Municipal Airport</a>, (SDM) (formerly East Field, NAAS Otay Mesa, and NAAS Brown Field)</li>
</ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Communities">Communities</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=San_Diego_County,_California&amp;action=edit&amp;section=42" title="Edit section: Communities">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:North_County_San_Diego.png"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1286" data-file-width="2000" height="141" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7a/North_County_San_Diego.png/220px-North_County_San_Diego.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7a/North_County_San_Diego.png/330px-North_County_San_Diego.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7a/North_County_San_Diego.png/440px-North_County_San_Diego.png 2x" width="220"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:North_County_San_Diego.png" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
<b><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/North_County" title="North County">North County</a></b> communities. Coastal cities are in dark blue, unincorporated coastal communities are in light blue. Inland cities are in dark yellow, unincorporated inland communities are in light yellow. Parts of northern San Diego are sometimes considered part of North County, as are much of the white areas north of the city.</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:East_County_San_Diego.png"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1286" data-file-width="2000" height="141" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/22/East_County_San_Diego.png/220px-East_County_San_Diego.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/22/East_County_San_Diego.png/330px-East_County_San_Diego.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/22/East_County_San_Diego.png/440px-East_County_San_Diego.png 2x" width="220"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:East_County_San_Diego.png" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
<b>East County</b> communities in red. In dark red are the cities and towns of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Santee,_CA" title="Santee, CA">Santee</a> and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/El_Cajon,_CA" title="El Cajon, CA">El Cajon</a> which mark the western edge of East County. Unincorporated communities are in light red, including <a href="/wiki/Lakeside,_California" title="Lakeside, California">Lakeside</a> and <a href="/wiki/Alpine,_California" title="Alpine, California">Alpine</a>.</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:South_Bay_Communities_San_Diego.png"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1286" data-file-width="2000" height="141" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4d/South_Bay_Communities_San_Diego.png/220px-South_Bay_Communities_San_Diego.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4d/South_Bay_Communities_San_Diego.png/330px-South_Bay_Communities_San_Diego.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4d/South_Bay_Communities_San_Diego.png/440px-South_Bay_Communities_San_Diego.png 2x" width="220"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:South_Bay_Communities_San_Diego.png" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
<b>South Bay</b> communities of San Diego County. The cities and towns of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/National_City,_CA" title="National City, CA">National City</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Chula_Vista,_CA" title="Chula Vista, CA">Chula Vista</a>, and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Imperial_Beach,_CA" title="Imperial Beach, CA">Imperial Beach</a> are in dark orange. The unincorporated community of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Bonita,_CA" title="Bonita, CA">Bonita</a> is in light orange. <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/San_Ysidro,_San_Diego,_California" title="San Ysidro, San Diego, California">San Ysidro</a> and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Otay_Mesa,_San_Diego,_California" title="Otay Mesa, San Diego, California">Otay Mesa</a>, neighborhoods of the city of San Diego, are in pink.</div>
</div>
</div>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Indian_reservations">Indian reservations</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=San_Diego_County,_California&amp;action=edit&amp;section=46" title="Edit section: Indian reservations">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>San Diego County has 18 federally recognized <a href="/wiki/Indian_reservation" title="Indian reservation">Indian reservations</a>, more than any other county in the United States.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-84"><a href="#cite_note-84">[80]</a></sup> Although they are typical in size to other Indian reservations in California (many of which are termed "<a href="/wiki/Rancher%C3%ADa" title="Ranchería">Rancherías</a>"), they are relatively tiny by national standards,<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (January 2010)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup> and all together total 200.2 square miles (518.5 km²) of area.</p>
<div class="div-col columns column-width" style="-moz-column-width: 20em; -webkit-column-width: 20em; column-width: 20em;">
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Barona_Group_of_Capitan_Grande_Band_of_Mission_Indians" title="Barona Group of Capitan Grande Band of Mission Indians">Barona Indian Reservation</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Campo_Indian_Reservation" title="Campo Indian Reservation">Campo Indian Reservation</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Capitan_Grande_Reservation" title="Capitan Grande Reservation">Capitan Grande Reservation</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Ewiiaapaayp_Band_of_Kumeyaay_Indians" title="Ewiiaapaayp Band of Kumeyaay Indians">Ewiiaapaayp Indian Reservation</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Inaja_Band_of_Diegueno_Mission_Indians" title="Inaja Band of Diegueno Mission Indians">Inaja and Cosmit Indian Reservation</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jamul_Indian_Village" title="Jamul Indian Village">Jamul Indian Village</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/La_Jolla_Band_of_Luiseno_Indians" title="La Jolla Band of Luiseno Indians">La Jolla Indian Reservation</a></li>

<li><a href="/wiki/Los_Coyotes_Band_of_Cahuilla_and_Cupeno_Indians" title="Los Coyotes Band of Cahuilla and Cupeno Indians">Los Coyotes Indian Reservation</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Manzanita_Band_of_Diegueno_Mission_Indians" title="Manzanita Band of Diegueno Mission Indians">Manzanita Indian Reservation</a></li>

<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Rincon_Indian_Reservation" title="Rincon Indian Reservation">Rincon Indian Reservation</a></li>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Notes">Notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=San_Diego_County,_California&amp;action=edit&amp;section=49" title="Edit section: Notes">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="reflist" style="list-style-type: decimal;">
<ol class="references">
<li id="cite_note-PCT-RV-56"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-PCT-RV_56-0">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Percentage of registered voters with respect to total population. Percentages of party members with respect to registered voters follow.</span></li>
<li id="cite_note-LT-note-66"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-LT-note_66-0">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Only larceny-theft cases involving property over $400 in value are reported as property crimes.</span></li>
</ol>
</div>
<div class="reflist" style="list-style-type: lower-alpha;">
<ol class="references">
<li id="cite_note-24"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-24">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Mean monthly maxima and minima (i.e. the highest and lowest temperature readings during an entire month or year) calculated based on data at said location from 1981 to 2010.</span></li>
<li id="cite_note-26"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-26">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Official precipitation records for San Diego were kept at the Weather Bureau Office in downtown from October 1850 to December 1859 at the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mission_San_Diego" title="Mission San Diego">Mission San Diego</a> and from November 1871 to June 1939 and a variety of buildings at downtown, and at San Diego Int'l (Lindbergh Field) since July 1939.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-25"><a href="#cite_note-25">[24]</a></sup> Temperature records, however, only date from October 1874. For more information on data coverage, see <a class="external text" href="http://threadex.rcc-acis.org/" rel="nofollow">ThreadEx</a></span></li>
</ol>
</div>
